lexeme: Riemukaari

###  Riemukaari₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Riemukaari* (FIXME)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  24
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  ORG
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
